SQL> SELECT p.country_name, f.year, SUM(f.co2)
  2  FROM COUNTRIES p, FACTS f, AGE_GROUPS a
  3  WHERE p.id_country = f.id_country AND f.id_age_group = a.id_age_group AND a.age_group = 'TOTAL' AND f.co2 IS NOT NULL
  4  GROUP BY CUBE(p.country_name,f.year);
